<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fiddler.html>fiddler</a> (18066)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fiþelere</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fiþelere</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fiþele</i>.  <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fiddle</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fiddler.html>fiddler</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fiddlers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>One</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:who.html>who</a> plays <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> fiddle.</li>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> burrowing <a href = vnd.unilang:crab.html>crab</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genus.html>genus</a> <i>Gelasimus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:many.html>many</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:species.html>species</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:male.html>male</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:claw.html>claw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:very.html>very</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:much.html>much</a> enlarged, <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:often.html>often</a> holds <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:position.html>position</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:similar.html>similar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:musician.html>musician</a> holds <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> fiddle.</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:field.html>field</a> (467)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***fier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fier.html>fier</a> (14252)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:fier.html>fier</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fiksen.html>fiksen</a> (43798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fix.html>fix</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixen.html>fixen</a></i>, borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixen.html>fixe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fastened; <a href = vnd.unilang:fixed.html>fixed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fīxus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">immovable; steady; <a href = vnd.unilang:stable.html>stable</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:fixed.html>fixed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fīgere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drive.html>drive</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:stick.html>stick</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:fasten.html>fasten</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰeygʷ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jab.html>jab</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:stick.html>stick</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:set.html>set</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixen.html>fixen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixeren.html>fixeren</a></i>.
